normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...a <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">fundamental</strong></em></span> battle in the show was the jack/locke dynamic.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">本剧最<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">主要的</strong>矛盾</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6101852" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKfGGicBC2FtnAJwEENqsx2N9IOOF39d6uADn8ibegm0OqZMrcjVZy1C49pCXTh6icSFmkBGQSeuQefuQ/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《迷失》</span></p><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">...the <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">fundamental</strong></em></span> basic data can be traced to individual chromosomes.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">这些<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">基本的</strong>数据都能追溯到特定的染色体上。 </span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6175926" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKfGGicBC2FtnAJwEENqsx2N9gZowM7ZdYSUXCHKLF7qkeKibN7oNoyt4kbpBVHt3n7RO6QZFRl0yMKw/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《机器之心》</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">5. </em><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">*</em>se</strong><strong>e除了最普通的“看见”的释义之外，还有一个比较重要但常常不注意的释义，就是“留心、留神、设法办到、负责使之发生”。如果是这个释义，要采取see that...或者see to it that...的结构，that后面的从句的时态按情况用直陈式（不用虚拟式）一般现在时或一般过去时。</strong><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"></em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链儿：see to it that...  确保...发生、设法办到某事</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">= to make sure that…</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Can you <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">see to it that </strong></em></span>the fax goes this afternoon?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">保证</strong>今天下午就把传真发出去，行吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">See to it that</strong></em></span> everything is ready by 5 p. m.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你要把一切在下午五点以前<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">办好</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句</span></strong>：...trying to <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">see to it that</strong></em></span> <span style="text-decoration: underline;">each and every one</span> can find his or her place.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...努力<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">确保</strong>每个人都能找到自己的位置。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句</strong></span>：<span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">See to it that </strong></em></span>you be not misled.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">确保</strong>你不会被误导。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I can<span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong><em> see to it that, </em></strong></span>that never…happened.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我可以<strong>保证</strong>那永远…不会发生。</p></section><section with擅长于和…打交道，对…有办法</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He's very good with children. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他对孩子很有一套。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2. a sense of direction有方向感</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We are looking for somebody with a clear sense of direction. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们想找一个有明确目标的人。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.automatically </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˌɔːtəˈmætɪkli $ ˌɒː-/adv.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">自动地；机械地；without thinking about what you are doing无意识地adj.不经思索的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Of course I automatically said yes.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当然，我不自觉地就答应了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4. fairly </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈfeəli $ ˈferli/ adv. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">more than a little, but much less than very一定地;相当地;公平合理地;公正地;(用以强调)简直，竟然</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Both ships are fairly new.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">两艘船都还比较新。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5. navigator </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> /ˈnævəɡeɪtə $ -tər/ n.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(飞机、船舶等上的)航行者，航海者，驾驶员，领航员an officer on a ship or aircraft who plans which way it should go when it is travelling from one place to another</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He became an RAF navigator during the war.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他在战争期间成为皇家空军的领航员。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> learning some vocabulary along the way. I'm Alice an<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> joining me today is Neil. Welcome, Neil.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">大家好，欢迎收听本期</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">BBC</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">英语六分钟。在本期节目中，我们会看一个新闻故事，同时学习一些新的词汇和短语。我是爱丽丝，今天和我一起主持节目的是尼尔。你好，尼尔。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Hi there, Alice.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">你好，爱丽丝。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Now, Neil are you goo<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> with maps?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">尼尔</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">,</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">你善于使用地图吗？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Good with maps? You mean – a<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">m I</span></span> goo<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> reading maps?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">善于使用地图？你是说我擅长看地图吗？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Yes. Can you fin<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d you</span></span>r way t<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">o a</span></span> place you want to go to just by looking a<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t a</span></span> map?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">对，你只通过看地图就能找到你想去的地方吗？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">We<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ll, a</span></span>ctually I need a map. Because I use<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> to think I ha<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span> great sen<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">se o</span></span>f direction bu<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> now I have to admit I’ve got a terrible sen<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">se o</span></span>f direction. I almost always wal<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">k i</span></span>n the wrong direction automatically, so I nee<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span> map.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我确实需要看地图。因为过去我自以为方向感很好，但现在我不得不承认自己的方向感的确很差。我经常不自觉地就走错路了，所以我需要一张地图来指导方向。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">You nee<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span> map. Well I like to think I'<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">m a</span></span> fairly good navigator – that's someone who finds or plots the way. Bu<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> wha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> if the map is wrong? I once walk<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ed a</span></span>roun<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span> town for a whole hour using a map I'd downloaded from the internet, and then I realise<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> the map I was using was completely wrong.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">你需要地图来指导方向。我却是一个很好的导航员</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">——</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">发现并规划路线的人。但如果地图是错的会怎么样呢？曾经有一次我用一张在网上下载的地图做向导，却在小镇上转了整整一个小时，后来才发现我用的那张地图完全是错的。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Oh dear, it does happen.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">哦，亲爱的，这种事情时有发生。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Yes, i<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> does.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">确实如此。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">THE place where they had met the Fauns was, of course, Dancing Lawn itself, and here Caspian and his friends remained till the night of the great Council. To sleep under the stars, to drink nothing but well water and to live chiefly on nuts and wild fruit, was a strange experience for Caspian after his bed with silken sheets in a tapestried chamber at the castle, with meals laid out on gold and silver dishes in the anteroom, and attendants ready at his call. But he had never enjoyed himself more. Never had sleep been more refreshing nor food tasted more savoury, and he began already to harden and his face wore a kinglier look.      </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们遇见羊怪的草坪，正是著名的跳舞场。经过商量，凯斯宾和他的朋友们决定留下，等待那盛大集会的来临。他们唱井水止渴，吃野果充饥，晚上就露宿在满天星斗之下口这一切对凯斯宾来说真是新鲜极了。虽然早已习惯了挂满壁毯的卧室，温暖柔软的被褥，以及山珍海昧、奴仆成群的王宫生活，王子从来没有像现在这样快活，晚上从来不曾睡得这么香甜，胃口也从来没有这么好。他已经变得坚强起来，不论气质还是仪表都俨然是一国之君的样子。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：朱迪，你已经算出来我们要花多少钱了吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：噢，是的。李，根据我们的行程宋看，总数不会少于1 3000元。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：什么？这么多！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：先坐下吧。我给你看看我们的预算清单。首先，我们在交通上要花将近4000元。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：啊，交通费在预算中总会占很大一部分。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：然后我们住这旅馆要花一大笔钱。如果想省钱，我们可以不选择这么好的旅馆。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：嗯，但我担心一旦我们选择便宜的旅馆，件宿条件也会跟着变得很差。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：这样的话，我们可以选择青年旅馆。那是一个不错的选择，干净又经济。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Judy, have you ever made out how much money shall we spend?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Oh, yeah. The total amount is no less than 13.000 RMB, according to our itinerary.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: What? That's too much.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Sit down. I'll show you the list of our financial budget. First of all, it is nearly 4,000 RMB that we should spend in transportation.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Ah, the transportation fee always takes a great part in the budget.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Then we must pay a large amount of money for the hotel. But if we want to save money, we can choose a hotel which is not so good.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Hmm, what I'm fearful of is that the accommodation will also deteriorate once we choose a cheaper hotel.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: In that case, we can choose the Youth Hotel. It's a good choice, clean and economic.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Want to drink him under the table? Well…you can never do. He got a hollow leg, you know.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你像灌醉他？他可是__________，从来没有醉过。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">海量</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;text-align: justify;font-size: 16px;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所以，之后想要表达“<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">这片，这个地方，这一带</strong>”的时候，考虑一下“(the) neck of the woods”～</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">② risk...neck (=risk my life) 冒险</strong><section 麻烦</strong><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">✔ These little kids are really <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">pains in the neck</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“wood” 除了可以表示“木头，木材”的含义之外，还可以表示：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">an area of trees, smaller than a forest <br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>树林；林地</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;">a large wood 一大片树林</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;">a walk in the woods 在树林中散步</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">not see the wood for the trees</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">( BrE) ( NAmE not see the ˌforest for the ˈtrees ) to not see or understand the main point about sth, because you are paying too much attention to small details 见树不见林</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I think you and your wife have been short-sighted. You <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">can't see the woods for the trees</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我觉得你和你爱人都目光短浅。你们一直是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">只见树木，不见森林</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 0.5em;margin-bottom: 0.5em;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">not out of the woods</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">(informal) not yet free from difficulties or problems 尚未摆脱困境；尚未渡过难关</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: improving but they're <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">not out of the woods yet</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">情况正有所改善, 但她们<strong 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">[uncountable ] people or things that have become useless or unnecessary in an organization 冗员；废物/ 枯木</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He took out his knife and cut away some of the <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">dead wood</strong> from the rose trees.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他掏出小刀割去这些玫瑰枝干上的一些<strong style="box-sizing: by </strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 16px;box-sizing: and say hello.</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: none;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">a culture of XX</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">看到 “a culture of XX” 不要第一反应认为是“……的文化”这个含义，这个语境中，culture的含义是这样的：</span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">释义：</p><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">[countable ] ( biology 生 ) ( medical 医 ) a group of cells or bacteria, especially one taken from a person or an animal and grown for medical or scientific study, or to produce food; the process of obtaining and growing these cells</em></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">培养细胞；培养菌；（为医疗、科研或食品生产而作细胞或细菌的）培养</em></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例如：</p><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">a culture of</strong> cells from the tumour 肿瘤细胞<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">的培养</strong>Yogurt is made from active <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">cultures</strong>. 酸奶是由活性<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">培养菌</strong>制成的。</section><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">但是 “a culture of XX”的确可以表示“……的文化”这个含义的哈~</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">比如：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We have to have <span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">a culture of </strong></span>creativity, of imagination, to keep improving.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们需要有创造力、想象力<span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">的文化</strong></span>才能一直进步<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">。</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span rgb(71, 193, 168);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">能让XX变得滑稽好笑🤪 真的难，但不管怎么说，你做到了！</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">It's hard to make that dull story hilarious, and yet somehow you do it.</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">把无趣的故事描述得滑稽可笑真是难，但不管怎么着，你确实成功了。</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"> a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">hilarious</strong> joke/story <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">令人捧腹的</strong>笑话╱故事</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: 193, 168);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">generate 产生，创造<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">generative 有生产力的，能生产的</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">de-</strong>generative 退化的</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">这里我们来看一个词缀：</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">de- / diː ; NAmE diː / </strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">PREFIX ( in verbs and related nouns, adjectives and adverbs 构成动词及相关的名词、形容词和副词 )</em></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">① the opposite of …的反义</em></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">decentralization 权力分散</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">② removing sth 除掉；去掉；取消</em></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">to defrost the refrigerator (= remove layers of ice from it) 给冰箱除霜</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所以，之后想要表达“<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">这片，这个地方，这一带</strong>”的时候，考虑一下“(the) neck of the woods”～</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“wood” 除了可以表示“木头，木材”的含义之外，还可以表示：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">an area of trees, smaller than a forest <br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>树林；林地</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;">a large wood 一大片树林</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;">a walk in the woods 在树林中散步</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">not see the wood for the trees</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">( BrE) ( NAmE not see the ˌforest for the ˈtrees ) to not see or understand the main point about sth, because you are paying too much attention to small details 见树不见林</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I think you and your wife have been short-sighted. You <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">can't see the woods for the trees</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我觉得你和你爱人都目光短浅。你们一直是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">只见树木，不见森林</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 0.5em;margin-bottom: 0.5em;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;width: 85%;border-width: 0.3em;border-style: solid;border-color: white;box-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 0.2em 0.2em 0.5em;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;height: auto !important;"><img data-ratio="0.6571429" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKcD8oUNicofIbicyn7fn3ibibuISBxBfnhCibMDiagq5VRQLibU4uCcWGe5iaZgSPgBI8BCNRKKQdFxzFPnzg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="700" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">not out of the woods</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">(informal) not yet free from difficulties or problems 尚未摆脱困境；尚未渡过难关</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The situation's improving but they're <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">not out of the woods yet</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">情况正有所改善, 但她们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">仍未摆脱困境</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">dead wood</strong><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">[uncountable ] people or things that have become useless or unnecessary in an organization 冗员；废物/ 枯木</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He took out his knife and cut away some of the <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">dead wood</strong> from the rose trees.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他掏出小刀割去这些玫瑰枝干上的一些<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">枯枝</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 0.5em;margin-bottom: 0.5em;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;width: 85%;border-width: 0.3em;border-style: solid;border-color: white;box-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 0.2em 0.2em 0.5em;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;height: auto !important;"><img data-ratio="0.6666667" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKcD8oUNicofIbicyn7fn3ibibuIQNtKfuEvPeuvg6v5ypWsRJQrRB3Bh2ibNeyGia7hicAY47y4v2YQPRFCA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1050" border-box;">She cleared out the <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">dead wood</strong> as soon as she took over the company.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她接手公司后就清理了一些<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">冗员</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0% 0px;text-align: left;justify-content: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: style="font-size: 16px;color: rgb(5, 5, 5);font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Part 3 其他表达</strong></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: -12px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 12px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(254, 230, 213);border-width: 0px;border-radius: 81px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">pop by </strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">顺道拜访</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;text-decoration: none;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: none;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">I just thought we knew each other well enough to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">pop by</strong> and say hello.</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: none;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">我还以为我们熟到能<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">过来转转</strong>，打个招呼呢。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">a culture of XX</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">看到 “a culture of XX” 不要第一反应认为是“……的文化”这个含义，这个语境中，culture的含义是这样的：</span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">释义：</p><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">[countable ] ( biology 生 ) ( medical 医 ) a group of cells or bacteria, especially one taken from a person or an animal and grown for medical or scientific study, or to produce food; the process of obtaining and growing these cells</em></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">培养细胞；培养菌；（为医疗、科研或食品生产而作细胞或细菌的）培养</em></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例如：</p><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">a culture of</strong> cells from the tumour 肿瘤细胞<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">的培养</strong>Yogurt is made from active <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">cultures</strong>. 酸奶是由活性<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">培养菌</strong>制成的。</section><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">但是 “a culture of XX”的确可以表示“……的文化”这个含义的哈~</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">比如：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We have to have <span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">a culture of </strong></span>creativity, of imagination, to keep improving.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们需要有创造力、想象力<span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">的文化</strong></span>才能一直进步<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">。</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);box-sizing: border-box;">It's hard to make XX hilarious, and yet somehow you do it.</span></strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">能让XX变得滑稽好笑🤪 真的难，但不管怎么说，你做到了！</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">It's hard to make that dull story hilarious, and yet somehow you do it.</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">把无趣的故事描述得滑稽可笑真是难，但不管怎么着，你确实成功了。</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"> a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">hilarious</strong> joke/story <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">令人捧腹的</strong>笑话╱故事</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">degenerative </strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">退化</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">generate 产生，创造<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">generative 有生产力的，能生产的</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">de-</strong>generative 退化的</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">这里我们来看一个词缀：</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">de- / diː ; NAmE diː / </strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">PREFIX ( in verbs and related nouns, adjectives and adverbs 构成动词及相关的名词、形容词和副词 )</em></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">① the opposite of …的反义</em></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">decentralization 权力分散</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">② removing sth 除掉；去掉；取消</em></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">to defrost the refrigerator (= remove layers of ice from it) 给冰箱除霜</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">brain maladies </strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">脑部疾病</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">It's really sad to be diagnosed with <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">brain maladies</strong>.</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">被诊断出患有<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">脑部疾病</strong>，真的是太惨了。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">that's fun to do </strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">做……感到快乐</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">That's fun to</strong> have such a nice dinner.</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">如此丰盛的晚餐<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">真是太开心了</strong>！</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">get XX off the table</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">把XX从桌子上上拿下去</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Get your little cute rabbit off the table.</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">把你那小兔子从桌子上拿下去。</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">change the subject</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">转换话题</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">It's the right time to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">change the subject</strong>.</span></p><p 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">suspicious</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">音标：/ səˈspɪʃəs / </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：feeling that sb has done sth wrong, illegal or dishonest, without having any proof</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中文释义：感觉可疑的；怀疑的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They became suspicious of his behaviour and contacted the police. 他们开始觉得他行为可疑，便报了警。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a suspicious look 怀疑的神情</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You have a very suspicious mind (= you always think that people are behaving in an illegal or dishonest way). 你疑心很重。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Legendary</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英式发音：/ ˈledʒəndri / 美式发音：/ ˈledʒənderi  / </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：very famous and talked about a lot by people, especially in a way that shows admiration</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中文释义：非常著名的；享有盛名的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a legendary figure 大名鼎鼎的人物</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the legendary Bob Dylan 名扬四海的鲍勃 · 迪伦</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Her patience and tact are legendary. 她的耐心与老练是出了名的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：mentioned in stories from ancient times</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中文释义：传奇的；传说的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> legendary heroes 传奇故事中的英雄</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vessel </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">音标：/ ˈvesl / </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：a large ship or boat</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中文释义：大船；轮船</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> ocean-going vessels 远洋轮船</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(188, 132, 37);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgba(122, 120, 124, 0.91);font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">（请务必听写后校对） </span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">橙色弱读</span></span></p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(206, 169, 203);padding: 10px;box-shadow: rgb(204, 204, 204) 2.6px 2.6px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">Tuesday</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;color: rgb(9, 9, 9);line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="line-height: 19px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">An<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d i</span></span>n 6 Minu<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">te E</span></span>nglish today, we'll be hearing abou<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t </span></span>an island <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">tha<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t h</span></span>as </em>appear<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ed o</span></span>n maps for several years, but which people now realise has never existed at all!</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">确实如此。在今天的节目中，我们将听到一个关于一个小岛的故事，这个岛屿在地图上存在了数年之久，但近期人们才发现它根本就不存在。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Aha, this is the famous Sandy Island <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">near</em> Australia.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">这就是澳大利亚附近著名的桑迪岛。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Yes, it's all very suspicious! And, Neil, <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">as we're </em>talking about islands, my question for you today is about a legendary island whi<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ch i</span></span>s supposed to have sunk into the ocean thousand<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s o</span></span>f years ago. Wa<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s i</span></span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> called: a) Pacifica b) Atlantis, or c) Oceana</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">没错，这个岛屿确实很可疑！尼尔，既然今天我们谈论的是岛屿，那么我的问题是：有一个传说中的岛屿，数千年前就沉入海底了，这个岛屿是：</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">a) </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">帕西菲卡</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> b) </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">亚特兰蒂斯</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">, </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">还是</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> c) </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">奥希阿纳</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Well, I will ha<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ve a </span></span>think abou<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> that an<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> tell you a<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> the en<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d o</span></span>f the programme.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">让我想一下，我会在节目最后再告诉你我的答案。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">OK, as usual we'll find out what the answer is a<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> the end. Now let's hear more about Sandy Island – the island that never was! Maria Seton from the University of Sydney in Australia <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">was on an </em>expedition<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"> in the </em>sea between Australia and New Caledonia.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">好的，和往常一样，我们在节目的最后再揭晓答案。现在我们就进一步了解一下桑迪岛</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">——</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">一个从来就不存在的岛屿。来自澳大利亚悉尼大学的玛丽亚</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">·</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">希顿进行了一次从澳大利亚到新喀里多尼亚（位于南太平洋）的海上探险。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">We were</span></em><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> actually ou<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> in the Eastern Coral Sea conducting a scientific research expedition and <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">when we were </em>approaching <span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">the area of </span></span>this supposed island, we saw that our scientific maps showed there was an island there, an<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> ye<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> the navigation charts on board the vessel showed that we had a water depth<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"> of </em>1, 400 metres.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我们当时其实是在东部珊瑚海进行科学研究考察，我们准备向这个本以为存在的岛屿靠近时，我们的科学地图上显示那里有一个岛屿，但我们船上的导航图却显示那里是</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">1400</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">米深的水域。</span></p><p style="line-height: 19px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Twilight was coming on as they rowed slowly up the windings of Glasswater Creek - a twilight which deepened as the banks drew closer together and the overhanging trees began almost to meet overhead. It was very quiet in here as the sound of the sea died away behind them; they could even hear the trickle of the little streams that poured down from the forest into Glasswater.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当他们慢慢划过清水湾的时候，夜幕已经降临——随着海岸一点点靠近，暮色也越来越浓，河岸上伸出来的树枝不时碰到头上。大海的声音在他们身后渐渐消失了，这里非常安静，甚至能听见潺潺的小溪从森林里流向清水湾。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：你的脸色不太好。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：我觉得不太舒服，我感冒了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：你是因为天气不好病了吗？这几天的天气真让人受不了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：可不是嘛！最近很冷，风又大。你喜欢这儿的天气吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：不太喜欢，但是我已经习惯了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：嗅，我秋天要到纽约去游玩，那儿的天气怎么样？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：天气不很好，风多又干燥。那里是大陆性气候，终年干燥。秋天通常是纽约一年中最好的季节。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：那儿的秋天很冷吗？我需要带很多保暖衣服吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：不用，那时不会太冷。你只需带些毛衣，加上几件外套和衬衣就行了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: You don't look very well.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I'm not feeling too well. I've caught a cold.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Is it because of the bad weather? It's been really miserable for the past tew days.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Hasn't it! It's been cold and windy recently. Do you like the weather here?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Not really, but I've got used it now.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Oh, I'm going for a trip New York this autumn. What's the weather like in New York?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Not quite good. It's windy and dry. We have got continental climate there. It's dry all the year round. Usually autumn is the best season of the year In New York.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Is it cold in autumn there? Should I take any warm clothes with me?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: No, it isn't very cold at that time. You'll only need some light wool clothing with some jackets and shirts.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She insisted that she would not marry herself off to a hayseed, no matter how rich he was.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她说她决不会嫁给一个____________，不管他多有钱。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">乡巴佬</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;font-size: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你拿这两个包，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">剩下的</strong>我来拿。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">His latest novel is a cut above<span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> the rest</strong></em></span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他最近出版的小说<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">比其他的</strong>小说<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">都好</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p figure it out <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">along the way</strong></em></span>.</p><p
