tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> there was, was 1, 400 meters of water.</span></p><p Bu<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> how coul<span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span>ll maps make the same mistake?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">真有意思。但怎么可能所有的地图都犯同样的错误呢？</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 19px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It was certainly an awesome place, a round green hill on top of another hill, long since grown over with trees, and one little, low doorway leading into it. The tunnels inside were a perfect maze till you got to know them, and they were lined and roofed with smooth stones, and on the stones, peering in the twilight, Caspian saw strange characters and snaky patterns, and pictures in which the form of a Lion was repeated again and again. It all seemed to belong to an even older Narnia than the Narnia of which his nurse had told him.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这是个僻静的地方，一个馒头状的绿色土丘，坐落在小山顶上。在大树的浓阴下，有一条蜿蜒的小道，直通土丘的中心。堡垒里面结构复杂，对不熟悉它的人来说，简直是个迷宫。里面四壁全是用光滑的石头砌起来的。借着昏暗的光线，凯斯宾看到石壁上刻着一些奇形怪状的文字和蛇形花纹，还有许多有关狮子的图画。这一切都在向他表明那个古老而又神秘的纳尼亚确实存在着。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：这些是您的包吗，先生？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：是的，没错。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：您有什么东西要申报吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：没有，我只带了些衣服之类的东西。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：您到这里来干什么？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：来这儿出差。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：我知道了。您介意把这个打开看看吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：完全不介意。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：这个包裹里面是什么？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：是给我朋友的礼物。玻璃花瓶之类的东西。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：带烟了吗？酒呢？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：带了200支香烟，但没带酒。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Are these your bags, sir?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yes, that's right.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Have you anything to declare?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: No, I've only got some clothes and things like that.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: What's the purpose of your visit?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I'm here on business.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I see. Would you mind opening this one?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Not at all.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: What's inside the package?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Presents for some of my friends. They're glass vases and so on.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Got any cigarettes? Spirits?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I've got 200 cigarettes, but I haven't got any spirits.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He’s an eager beaver, never staying idle.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他特别________，从来没有闲着的时候。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">勤快</p><p style="white-space: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">① advice为名词；advise为动词</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">② advice 是不可数名词，不能说*an advice，要说 a piece of advice。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">③ advice 是一般的、不正式、非专业的建议或劝告；</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: 则是专家就个人问题提供的专业咨询。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: I 'd be happy every day of my life if I had a group of elegant friends like that.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">So how does someone join a club like that?</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Oh,well, you have to be nominated by a current member. I met her at your father's clinic.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Talk to her.I bet she'd help you.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Oh, I don't know. I've introduced myself to her a few times, but she never seems to remember me. Guess I'm just not very memorable.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I say give it one more try.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Nah, I'd just be wasting my time.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">But what's that old saying ? 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-width: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);border-radius: 1px;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgba(197, 227, 211, 0.34);padding: 0px 10px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;align-self: stretch;margin: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;justify-content: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 30px;height: 40px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-radius: 0% 100px 100px 0%;border-width: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(160, 211, 192);padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 8px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">01</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: stretch;height: auto;padding: 8px 0px 0px 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: rgb(83, 118, 105);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">grab a bite</p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;color: rgb(83, 118, 105);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"></em></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Grab a bite 吃点东西</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英解：to get something to eat quickly</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“Grab”是“抓取”的意思；而“bite”原本是“咬”的意思，但在这边是当名词用，指“吃的东西”。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所以，“grab a bite”可以用来指“匆匆忙忙、简单吃点东西、随便吃点，垫垫肚子”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">As the train won't leave until one o'clock , we might as well <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">grab a bite</strong> at the snack bar.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">火车一点才开，咱们干脆去卖小吃的地方<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(83, 118, 105);box-sizing: border-box;">随便吃点儿什么东西吧</span></strong>。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);border-radius: 1px;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgba(197, 227, 211, 0.34);padding: 0px 10px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: border-box;">05</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: stretch;height: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">What's that old saying?</p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;color: rgb(83, 118, 105);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">老话怎么说来着？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(83, 118, 105);box-sizing: border-box;">What was that old saying, that cynical saying?</span></strong> "The husband is always the last to find out" .</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(83, 118, 105);box-sizing: border-box;">那句古话怎么说的</span></strong>，那句嘲弄人的古话？" 老婆都跑了，丈夫最后才知道。" </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;color: rgb(83, 118, 105);line-height: 1.8;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">补充一个The old saying goes...就是“老话常讲，古语有云”  As the old saying goes就是“正如老话说的那样”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(83, 118, 105);box-sizing: border-box;">As the old saying goes, </span></strong>failure teaches the success.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">按老话说，</strong>"失败教会了成功。"</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">But <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(83, 118, 105);box-sizing: border-box;">as the old saying goes,</span></strong> "when humans plan, God laughs."</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">正如老话所说，</strong>“人类一计划，上帝就发笑。”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;color: rgb(83, 118, 105);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(83, 118, 105);box-sizing: border-box;">不入虎穴，焉得虎子。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">venture 勇于做，冒险做；冒险尝试</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">venture XX 冒着...风险；冒着失去...的风险</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Nothing ventured, nothing gained.的结构是(If) nothing is ventured,nothing (will be) gained.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>这是一个条件状语从句.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-width: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);border-radius: 1px;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgba(197, 227, 211, 0.34);padding: 0px 10px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;align-self: stretch;margin: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;justify-content: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 30px;height: 40px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-radius: 0% 100px 100px 0%;border-width: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(160, 211, 192);padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 8px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">01</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: stretch;height: auto;padding: 8px 0px 0px 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: rgb(83, 118, 105);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">grab a bite</p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;color: rgb(83, 118, 105);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"></em></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Grab a bite 吃点东西</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英解：to get something to eat quickly</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“Grab”是“抓取”的意思；而“bite”原本是“咬”的意思，但在这边是当名词用，指“吃的东西”。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所以，“grab a bite”可以用来指“匆匆忙忙、简单吃点东西、随便吃点，垫垫肚子”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">As the train won't leave until one o'clock , we might as well <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">grab a bite</strong> at the snack bar.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">火车一点才开，咱们干脆去卖小吃的地方<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(83, 118, 105);box-sizing: border-box;">随便吃点儿什么东西吧</span></strong>。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);border-radius: 1px;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgba(197, 227, 211, 0.34);padding: 0px 10px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: border-box;">05</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: stretch;height: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">What's that old saying?</p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;color: rgb(83, 118, 105);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">老话怎么说来着？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(83, 118, 105);box-sizing: border-box;">What was that old saying, that cynical saying?</span></strong> "The husband is always the last to find out" .</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(83, 118, 105);box-sizing: border-box;">那句古话怎么说的</span></strong>，那句嘲弄人的古话？" 老婆都跑了，丈夫最后才知道。" </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;color: rgb(83, 118, 105);line-height: 1.8;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">补充一个The old saying goes...就是“老话常讲，古语有云”  As the old saying goes就是“正如老话说的那样”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(83, 118, 105);box-sizing: border-box;">As the old saying goes, </span></strong>failure teaches the success.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">按老话说，</strong>"失败教会了成功。"</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">But <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(83, 118, 105);box-sizing: border-box;">as the old saying goes,</span></strong> "when humans plan, God laughs."</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">正如老话所说，</strong>“人类一计划，上帝就发笑。”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;color: rgb(83, 118, 105);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(83, 118, 105);box-sizing: border-box;">不入虎穴，焉得虎子。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">venture 勇于做，冒险做；冒险尝试</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">venture XX 冒着...风险；冒着失去...的风险</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Nothing ventured, nothing gained.的结构是(If) nothing is ventured,nothing (will be) gained.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>这是一个条件状语从句.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.nautical </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英 /'nɔːtɪk(ə)l/ 美 /'nɔtɪkl/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 航海的，海上的；船员的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">nautical mile 海里（合1.852公里）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">nautical chart 航海图</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：Ships transiting U.S. waters are required to carry nautical charts,which they use to plan their routes for intended voyages.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.Google Earth</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">谷歌地球；谷歌地图</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.variety </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英 /və'raɪətɪ/ 美 /və'raɪəti/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 多样；种类；杂耍；变化，多样化</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a variety of / various 种种的；各种各样的； </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：We stock a wide variety of styles and sizes.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们有各种款式各种尺码的货品。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4.compile</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英 /kəm'paɪl/ 美 /kəm'paɪl/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 编译；编制；编辑；[图情] 汇编</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：The book took 10 years to compile.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这本书花了10年编写。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Compile与edit的区别</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">compile 指“编写”、“汇编”的意思。经收集有关资料加以组织后或“编写”、“汇编”出作品。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1) It takes years of hard work to compile a good dictionary.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">  编写一本好字典需要多年的辛勤工作。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">edit 指编辑他人的作品、尤指发表于报纸或刊物上的文章。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1)She is busy editing a volume of fairy tales of different countries for children.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她忙着编辑一册关于各国家孩子的童话故事。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5.spot</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt.发现</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：He failed to spot the error.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他没能发现这个错误。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(188, 132, 37);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">（请务必听写后校对） </span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">橙色弱读</span></span></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p 108, 10);box-sizing: border-box;">of</span></em> the sea, bu<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> easier to copy someo<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ne e</span></span>lse's map. Here's what the BBC's Duncan Kennedy say<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span>bou<span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">BBC</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">的邓肯</span><span style="font-size: i<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t a</span></span>ppear<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: mistakes coul<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> they le<span style="text-decoration: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">桑迪岛出现在标准地图上，航海地图上，甚至谷歌地图上。澳大利亚谷歌地图发言人表示，他们绘制地图时会采用很多参考资料，但这种情况也发生了变化。他们一直在建议大家，如果有人发现了类似的错误，请告知他们。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: tell them if they spo<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> similar mistakes on a<span 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Yes, things change! Even islands disappear sometimes – which brings me to the answer to your question a<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> the beginning of 6 Minu<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">te</span></span> English, Alice. I think I know the name of tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> legendary island you were talking about.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">确实，情况变了！岛屿有时候还会消失</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">——</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">这让我想到了在节目开始时你问我的问题。我想我知道你所说的那个传说中的岛屿的名字。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Ah yes, I ask<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ed y</span></span>ou if it was called: a. Pacifica, b. Atlantis or c. Oceana.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">是的，我的问题是这个岛屿是：</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">a) </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">帕西菲卡</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> b) </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">奥希阿纳</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Twang went the string. It was an excellent shot. The tiny apple shook as the arrow passed, and a leaf came fluttering down. Then Susan went to the top of the steps and strung her bow. She was not enjoying her match half so much as Edmund had enjoyed his; not because she had any doubt about hitting the apple but because Susan was so tenderhearted that she almost hated to beat someone who had been beaten already. The Dwarf watched her keenly as she drew the shaft to her ear. A moment later, with a little soft thump which they could all hear in that quiet place, the apple fell to the grass with Susan's arrow in it.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">只听嗖的一声，箭射出去了。这一箭射得很漂亮。箭到之处，小苹果摆了一摆，旁边的一片树叶飘然而落。下面轮到苏珊。她走到台阶上，拉开了弓。她对这场比赛并不感兴趣，这倒不是因为她对射中那只苹果没有信心，而是因为她心地善良，不愿意再去伤害一颗已经受到伤害的心。小矮人仔细观察着她如何把箭杆拉向耳边。刹那间，一声轻响，那苹果掉落在草地上，苏珊的箭插在正中间。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：全球航空公司订座中心。能帮您吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：是的，我来电确认机票。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：请问您叫什么名字？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：我叫李林。我事先已订了明天飞往伦敦的916次航班机票，下午2点离开纽约。可现在我想改变一下旅行日程。能不能将我的订票改到后天？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：当然可以，太太。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：后天同次航班有座吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：有，太太，您已重新确认10月25H飞往伦敦的916次航班机票，离开纽约的时间为下午2点钟。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Reservation Center, Global Airlines. Can I help you?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yes. I'm coming to confirm my ticker.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: May I have your name, please?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: My name is Li Lin, In fact, I have a reservation on Flight No.916 for London, leaving New York at 2:00 p.m. tomorrow. Now I'd like to make a change of my travel schedule. Is it possible to change my booking to the day after tomorrow?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Certainly, madam.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Do you have a seat available on the same flight the day after tomorrow?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Yes, madam. You are reconfirmed on Flight No. 916 for London, leaving New York at 2:00 p.m. on October 25.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Don’t you know she’s the one that would bite the hand that feeds her?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你难道不知道她是个__________的人？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">恩将仇报</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Books were invented only recently<span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> in the long history of</strong></em></span> mankind.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">书本也是近代<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">在</strong>人类<strong style="box-sizing: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. collaborate 合作，协作</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">col- 表示“与...一起，共同”</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">labor- 劳动</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">-ate 表动词“做，造成”</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">collaborate 共同劳动 → 合作</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链儿：collaborate with XX on.../in doing...</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She agreed to <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">collaborate with</strong></em></span> him in writing her biography.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她同意与他<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">合作</strong>撰写她的传记。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...you have to show you're willing to <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">collaborate </strong></em></span><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">with </strong></em></span>the Bureau.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你必须表现出你愿意跟局里好好<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">协作</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: most effectively 最善于随机应变的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">improvise v. 即兴作出；随机应变</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I forgot to bring my notes, so I had to <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">improvise</strong></em></span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我忘了带笔记，只好<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">临时发挥</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">an <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">improvised </strong></em></span>sketch</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">即兴</strong>素描</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(255, 104, 39);"><strong>★原声例句</strong></span>：They're not allowed to <span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><em><strong>improvise </strong></em></span>at all.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们根本不允许<strong>即兴</strong>发挥。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(255, 104, 39);"><strong>★原声例句</strong></span>：A wise person knows how to <span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><em><strong>improvise</strong></em></span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">聪明的人知道如何<strong>即兴发挥/随机应变</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...we messed up his plans. He had to <span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><em><strong>improvise</strong></em></span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">扰乱了他的计划，他只能<strong>临时改变</strong>计划。<br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《警察世家》</span></p><p style="white-space: 盛行；获胜；占...上风</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Justice will <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">prevail</strong></em></span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">正义终将<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">获胜</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Fortunately, common sense <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">prevailed</strong></em></span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;">看完视频之后，大家找到“<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">go-to place</strong>"这个表达了吗? go-to place就是“<strong>经常光顾的地方</strong>”，来看几个例句。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;">经常去</strong>哪个饭店吃饭？</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：That is not young people's <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">go-to place</strong>. 那里不是年轻人的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">聚集地</strong>。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;">“<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">go-to person</strong>"也是一个常用的表达，指：在某方面特别精通的人。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：He's the<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> go-to guy </strong>for questions about PPT. 他是PPT<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">大拿</strong></span>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section bringing the drama. 你是始作俑者</p></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 0 0 0%;align-self: flex-start;height: auto;margin: drama.</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: How did everything get to this. 好乱，事情怎么会变成这样。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Actually, <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">you are the one bringing the drama</strong>. 你才是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">始作俑者</strong>好吗。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: 100%;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;padding: 0px 4px;align-self: stretch;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;font-size: 19px;color: rgb(255, 255, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin: 0px 0%;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section Jim的情妇<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">踩着他前妻上的头上位的</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;background-color: rgb(181, 126, 121);min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;padding: 0px 4px;align-self: stretch;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;font-size: 19px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">04.</strong></p></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;background-color: rgba(213, 178, 122, 0.35);flex: 100 100 0%;height: auto;align-self: stretch;border-width: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin: 0px 0%;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: flex-start;height: auto;margin: 0px 0px 0px -1px;padding: 3px 5px 0px 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 3px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;line-height: 1.6;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px;color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">pursue XX. Hard. 猛烈的追求XX</p></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 0 0 0%;align-self: flex-start;height: auto;margin: 0px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: right;justify-content: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 10px;height: 10px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-left: 1px solid rgb(213, 178, 122);border-bottom-left-radius: 100%;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(213, 178, 122);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 0px;justify-content: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 6px;height: 6px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-left: 1px solid rgb(213, 178, 122);border-bottom-left-radius: 100%;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(213, 178, 122);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;background-color: rgb(254, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>：The point is, Antoine was a young, hot client, and he pursued Sylvie. Hard.</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：My father once<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> pursued my mother. Hard</strong>. 我爸曾经<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">猛烈地追求</strong>我妈。 </p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;background-color: rgb(181, 126, 121);min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;padding: 0px 4px;align-self: stretch;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;font-size: 19px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">05.</strong></p></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;background-color: rgba(213, 178, 122, 0.35);flex: 100 100 0%;height: auto;align-self: stretch;border-width: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin: 0px 0%;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: flex-start;height: auto;margin: 0px 0px 0px -1px;padding: 3px 5px 0px 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 3px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;line-height: 1.6;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px;color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's one thing to A. It's another thing to B. A是一回事，B就是另一回事了</p></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 0 0 0%;align-self: flex-start;height: auto;margin: 0px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: right;justify-content: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 10px;height: 10px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-left: 1px solid rgb(213, 178, 122);border-bottom-left-radius: 100%;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(213, 178, 122);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 0px;justify-content: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 6px;height: 6px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-left: 1px solid rgb(213, 178, 122);border-bottom-left-radius: 100%;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(213, 178, 122);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;background-color: rgb(254, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>：  It's one thing to cheat on your wife with your mistress. It's another thing to cheat on your mistress with  a young American.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：It's one thing to sneak out. It's another thing to tell a lie that you didn't sneak out. 你偷溜出去是一回事，偷溜出去还不承认吧就是另一回事了。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链精解</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;margin-bottom: 2px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0.6em;height: 0.6em;display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;margin-left: 6px;background-color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="width: 0.6em;height: 0.6em;display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;margin-left: 6px;opacity: 0.8;background-color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="width: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;">看完视频之后，大家找到“<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">go-to place</strong>"这个表达了吗? go-to place就是“<strong>经常光顾的地方</strong>”，来看几个例句。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：Which restaurant is your <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">go-to place</strong>? 你<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">经常去</strong>哪个饭店吃饭？</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：That is not young people's <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">go-to place</strong>. 那里不是年轻人的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">聚集地</strong>。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;">“<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">go-to person</strong>"也是一个常用的表达，指：在某方面特别精通的人。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：He's the<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> go-to guy </strong>for questions about PPT. 他是PPT<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">大拿</strong></span>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section How did everything get to this. 好乱，事情怎么会变成这样。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Actually, <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">you are the one Hard. 猛烈的追求XX</p></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 0 0 0%;align-self: flex-start;height: auto;margin: 0px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: right;justify-content: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 10px;height: 10px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-left: 1px solid rgb(213, 178, 122);border-bottom-left-radius: 100%;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(213, 178, 122);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 0px;justify-content: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 6px;height: 6px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-left: 1px solid rgb(213, 178, 122);border-bottom-left-radius: 100%;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(213, 178, 122);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;background-color: rgb(254, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>：The point is, Antoine was a young, hot client, and he pursued Sylvie. Hard.</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：My father once<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> pursued my mother. Hard</strong>. 我爸曾经<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">猛烈地追求</strong>我妈。 </p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;background-color: rgb(181, 126, 121);min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;padding: 0px 4px;align-self: stretch;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;font-size: 19px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">05.</strong></p></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;background-color: rgba(213, 178, 122, 0.35);flex: 100 100 0%;height: auto;align-self: stretch;border-width: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin: 0px 0%;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: flex-start;height: auto;margin: 0px 0px 0px -1px;padding: 3px 5px 0px 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 3px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;line-height: 1.6;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px;color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's one thing to A. It's another thing to B. A是一回事，B就是另一回事了</p></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 0 0 0%;align-self: flex-start;height: auto;margin: 0px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: right;justify-content: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 10px;height: 10px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-left: 1px solid rgb(213, 178, 122);border-bottom-left-radius: 100%;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(213, 178, 122);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 0px;justify-content: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 6px;height: 6px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-left: 1px solid rgb(213, 178, 122);border-bottom-left-radius: 100%;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(213, 178, 122);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;background-color: rgb(254, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>：  It's one thing to cheat on your wife with your mistress. It's another thing to cheat on your mistress with  a young American.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：It's one thing to sneak out. It's another thing to tell a lie that you didn't sneak out. 你偷溜出去是一回事，偷溜出去还不承认吧就是另一回事了。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(181, 126, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">看 <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">Emily in Paris </em>还可以学到哪些表达？都在下面的链接中哦。</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><a data-linktype="2" Claire</span></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;margin: 0px
