auto;align-self: center;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: center;height: auto;margin: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgb(226, 207, 188);height: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgba(222, 200, 200, 0.56);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></sectio</section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary &amp; Phrase</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1. 美剧常见英文缩写及用法 </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Gonna将要</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">gonna = going to表示即将做某件事，用法为：主语+ be gonna + 动词</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g：I am gonna go home.我要回家了</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Wanna 想要</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">wanna = want to / want a</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">用法:</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(1) I / you / we / they + wanna + 原形动词</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(2) He / she / it + wansta + 原形动词</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g：I wanna go home.  He/She/It wansta go home.我/TA想回家。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Gotta 必须</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">gotta = got to（have to）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">很多人会把gotta和gonna搞混，gotta跟going to无关，这个词相当于have to，用法是主语 + have/has + gotta +原形动词。有时候口语念得比较快，have/has可以被省略。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g：I've gotta go to bed.我必须要去睡了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g：Sam (has) gotta study hard to pass the exam.为了考试及格，山姆必须非常认真地念书。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Hafta 必须</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Hafta =Have to</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g：I hafta go. 我得走了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Coulda 本来可能</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Coulda =Could have</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g：You coulda told him the truth. 你本可以告诉他真相。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Shoulda 本来应该</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Shoulda = Should have</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g：You shoulda told him the truth.你本应该告诉他真相。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Woulda 本来可以</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Woulda =Would have</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g：You woulda told him the truth.你本可以告诉他真相。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Musta 一定是</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Musta =Must have</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一定是做了什么事</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g：We musta drank a lot last night.我们昨晚一定是喝了很多。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Sorta 一点点</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Sorta = Sort of = Kind of，复数为sortsa</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g：This movie is sorta cool. 这部电影有点酷。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Losta 很多</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">就是Lost of 的意思。（= A lot of）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">PS: 以上缩写念起来很顺，但是请记得它们是口语用法，不适合用在正式书写上。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2. trick </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK&amp;US/trɪk/ adj. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">used to deceive someone, either as a joke or form of entertainment or so that they makes a mistake捉弄的，戏弄的；恶作剧的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a trick question:a question which seems easy to answer but has a hidden difficulty一个捉弄人的问题,一个很容易让人上当的问题</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Word family: (noun) trick trickery trickster</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">           (adjective) tricky trick</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(verb)trick</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3. the name given to...给......起的名字</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g: “Troublemaker” was the name given to my friend, Peter, by his teachers.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“麻烦制造者”是我的朋友彼得的老师给他起的名字。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4. legendary </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/ˈledʒəndəri/ US/ˈledʒənderi/ adj. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">from a legend传说的，传奇的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g:Believed to be a legendary magic horse. 龙马是传说中的一种神马</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5. sunk </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK&amp;US/sʌŋk/ verb </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the past tense and past participle of sink </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to (cause something or someone to) go down below the surface or to the bottom of a liquid or soft substance（使）沉没；（使）陷入</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g: The Titanic was a passenger ship which sank (to the bottom of the ocean) in 1912.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">泰坦尼克号是1912年沉没（海底）的一艘客轮。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6.really do exist 真是存在(诙谐幽默）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g: Although we can't see these atoms, they really do exist.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">虽然我们看不见原子，但它们的确存在。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 181, 181);width: 99.9%;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="text-align: right;margin: -1.1em 0px border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 87);height: 1.2em;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style='border-radius: 100%;margin-left: -0.8em;display: inline-block;float: left;width: 1.6em;height: 1.6em;background-position: center 0px 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="padding-bottom: 8px;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="clear: none;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(188, 132, 37);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgba(122, 120, 124, 0.91);font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">（请务必听写后校对） </span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">橙色弱读</span></span></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(206, 169, 203);padding: 10px;box-shadow: rgb(204, 204, 204) 2.6px 2.6px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">Friday</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And soon the green, wooded coast of the island was falling away behind them, and its little bays and headlands were beginning to look flatter, and the boat was rising and falling in the gentle swell. The sea began to grow bigger around them and, in the distance, bluer, but close round the boat it was green and bubbly. Everything smelled salt and there was no noise except the swishing of water and the clop-clop of water against the sides and the splash of the oars and the jolting noise of the rowlocks. The sun grew hot.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">不久，那被密林覆盖的绿色小岛就被他们远远地抛在了身后，小船随着海浪上下颠簸着。周围的海域越来越辽阔，向远处望去，蓝蓝的海水一望无边，近处是小船荡起的碧绿的波浪，浪花在船边翻滚。空气中充满了海水的咸味。海上安静极了，只听到海水撞击船舷和船桨拍打水面的哗哗声，以及桨架发出的嘎吱声。天气开始热了起来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：需要帮忙吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：我和我的夫人想看看深圳、广州和珠海的名胜古迹，你能为我们安排一次旅行吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：你们想在这些城市待几天？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：嗯，三天。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：有一个三天的包价旅游。你们将在这磐城市单待满三天，是对整个城市进行游览的旅行。旅行路线包括像廿界之窗、中国民俗文化村、陈家祠、南越王墓、拱北市场等名胜古迹。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：听起来不错，这个旅行多少钱？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：每人200元。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：包括什么？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：包括机票、旅馆住宿和三餐。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：我们能让你们安排预订必要的飞机、饭店和旅程吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：是的，我们可以为你们做这一切。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：What can I do for you?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: My wife and I want to see the places of interest in Shenzhen, Guangzhou and Zhuhai. Can you arrange a tour for us?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: How long would you like to stay In these cities?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Well, three days.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: There is a three-day package tour. You will have 3 full days in the cities. It is a general tour of the cities. The itinerary includes the places of interest such as Window of the World, China Folk Culture Village. Chen Clan Academy, Southern Yue Tomb, and Gongbei Market.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: That sounds good. How much is the tour?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 200 yuan for each person.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: What does it include?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: It includes your air fare, your hotel accommodations and the meals.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Could we have you make all the necessary plane, hotel, and tour reservations?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Yes. we could do that for you.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">From the way she’s bowing and scraping in front of the boss, you’ll know what sort of person she is.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">从她在老板前___________地那个模样，你就知道她是个什么人了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">点头哈腰</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;text-align: auto;margin-top: -5px;width: 5px;height: 5px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(158, 154, 154);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">把你的答案留言吧，正确答案明天公布哦~</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">（点击题目即可回顾当期早读）</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="height: 16px;box-sizing: style="display: inline-block;color: transparent;clear: both;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.62);border-radius: 6px;overflow-wrap: break-word;box-sizing: border-box;margin: -13px 3px;padding: 12px;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653552674&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=74f7a7985f4113c557eab108f57c743f&amp;chksm=f7ebc0efc09c49f9e9b4063eaf5cf2072a84b7d906417ea0ad5e48e5f77b516ac190cad1ed67&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="1.Change will come when each of us has the courage to question our own fundamental values and beliefs. And then see to it that our actions lead to our best intentions.">1.Change will come when each of us has the courage to question our own fundamental values and beliefs. And then see to it that our actions lead to our best intentions.</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">see to it that... 不可以与哪一项替换？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A make sure that…   B see that...  C believe that...</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653552727&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=2897aae1f0af0ba1108e5c0975cc3af3&amp;chksm=f7ebc09ac09c498ca458bcc8090ce947ba347323d9c07db752702222fe9784699884a198dfe5&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="2.There's no use looking back or wonderingHow it could be now or might've beenAll this I know but still I can't find ways to let you go">2.There's no use looking back or wondering</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653552727&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=2897aae1f0af0ba1108e5c0975cc3af3&amp;chksm=f7ebc09ac09c498ca458bcc8090ce947ba347323d9c07db752702222fe9784699884a198dfe5&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="2.There's no use looking back or wonderingHow it could be now or might've beenAll this I know but still I can't find ways to let you go">How it could be now or might've been</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653552727&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=2897aae1f0af0ba1108e5c0975cc3af3&amp;chksm=f7ebc09ac09c498ca458bcc8090ce947ba347323d9c07db752702222fe9784699884a198dfe5&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="2.There's no use looking back or wonderingHow it could be now or might've beenAll this I know but still I can't find ways to let you go">All this I know but still I can't find ways to let you go</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">might've 包含几个音节？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A 1   B 2   C 3</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653552760&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=3e4ebe7f74f67ca61f03fb26fee5b810&amp;chksm=f7ebc0b5c09c49a38a3b44cf12cd0f5d93ba774c50c5db0351ea9c2e1b34d4abac8e219afb7a&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="3.The timing is never ever gonna be right, and you just have to do the thing and figure the rest out along the way.">3.The timing is never ever gonna be right, and you just have to do the thing and figure the rest out along the way.</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">timing 在句中的含义为：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A 时间   B 时机   C 定时</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653552790&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=b100e5ffe388468651451c0e420e4878&amp;chksm=f7ebc05bc09c494d547333e237b7428ac8363566876b485ad36b0cb8c3e2b65191ae13c10c08&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="4.My advice is to let your ambitions and your aspirations be your guide.">4.My advice is to let your ambitions and your aspirations be your guide.</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">句中最多包含几处连读？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A  6   B  7   C 8</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653552816&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=f11511276abb0315881506f3d28f0a5a&amp;chksm=f7ebc07dc09c496bae84692794fb3fdf9be4c4f2c49d3df146e56402172d4be0c73a32217c8b&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="5. In the long history of humankind(and animal kind, too), those who learned to collaborate and improvise most effectively have prevailed.">5. In the long history of humankind(and animal kind, too), those who learned to collaborate and improvise most effectively have prevailed.</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">those who 可以替换为：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A people who   B people  C whose</p></section></section><section style="height: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="height: 100%;width: 24px;float: left;border-bottom: 6px solid rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.62);border-left: 6px solid rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.62);border-top-color: rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.62);border-right-color: rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.62);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="height: 100%;width: 24px;float: right;border-bottom: 6px solid rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.62);border-right: 6px solid rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.62);border-top-color: rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.62);border-left-color: rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.62);box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: left;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="padding-bottom: 3px;display: -5px;padding: 5px 5px 2px;background-color: rgba(150, 195, 123, 0.44);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">本周知识点回想</p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: 160, 160);border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 0px 0px 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.     勤奋工作是成功的基础。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.     确保工作顺利完成是你的责任。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.     我想知道他们是如何使它变得有趣的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4.     我们必须找到一个办法去解决这些问题。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5.     你来得正是时候。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6.     我们一定要在过程中弄清楚。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7.     我是跟着感觉走。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">8.     她很聪明，但却缺乏远大志向。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">9.     聪明的人知道如何即兴发挥/随机应变。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">10.  幸而理智占了上风。</p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;font-size: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0.7em;height: 0.7em;margin-right: style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Gwen为你读</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 0.8;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 0.8em solid rgb(95, 156, 239);box-sizing: border-box;border-left: 0.7em solid transparent;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent;max-width: 100%;"></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;font-size: 18px;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"></strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">《沁园春·长沙》（1925）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">CHANGSHA</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Tune: “SPRING IN A PLEASURE GARDEN”</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1925 </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">背景音乐：</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">郭好为 - 在山间</span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;margin-left: 0px;"><img data-ratio="0.75" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKevZbB7CCGibeKgVRtja1Eicf3Njn21mmsPX1QWEFA6b85wqY2Pm3bDgviblk1MY07aquicSo5Picukpgw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">作者：毛泽东</p><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">翻译：许渊冲</p><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">朗读：Gwen</p><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">独立寒秋，湘江北去，橘子洲头。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">看万山红遍，层林尽染；漫江碧透，百舸争流。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">鹰击长空，鱼翔浅底，万类霜天竞自由。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">怅寥廓，问苍茫大地，谁主沉浮？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">携来百侣曾游，忆往昔峥嵘岁月稠。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">恰同学少年，风华正茂；书生意气，挥斥方遒。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">指点江山，激扬文字，粪土当年万户侯。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">曾记否，到中流击水，浪遏飞舟？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">In autumn cold alone stand I,</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Of Orange Islet at the head,</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Where River Xiang northward goes by.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I see hill on hill all in red,</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And wood on wood in a deep dye,</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The river green down to the bed,</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">In speed a hundred barges vie.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Far and wide eagles cleave the blue;</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Up and down fish in shallows glide:</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">All creatures strive for freedom under frosty skies.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Lost in immensity, I wonder who,</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Upon this boundless earth, decide</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">All beings’ fall and rise.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">With many friends I oft came here.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">How thick with salient days those bygone times appear!</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">When, students in the flower of our age,</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Our spirit bright was at its height,</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Full of the scholar’s noble rage,</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We criticized with all our might.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Pointing to stream and hill,</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Writing in blame or praise,</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We treat’d like dirt all mighty lords of olden days.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Do you remember still,</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Swimming mid-stream, we struck the waves to stay</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">That boats speeding their way?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;line-height: 0;width: 8%;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.1014151" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/pgC9Rudz9VUvUE94zFUGe0tW3EcqSmNNNugxQN543VLxANrGBtclBY9M6OSwUDMg4bUs7QQskngPAQzY3hfO8Q/640?wx_fmt=gif" data-type="gif" data-w="424" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;padding-left: 5px;padding-right: 5px;line-height: 1.2em;margin-bottom: 2px;font-size: 18px;color: rgb(121, 121, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-shadow: rgb(251, 197, 255) 2px 0px 2px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">关于作者</strong></span></p></section><section style="max-width: 100%;display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;line-height: 0;width: 8%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.0375" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/gDWI0uWrVSHvcvyjNUCSib0YBwdjrtGUuAwgpdte6GO7tYiadhbXiclBxNBW8GJohjw74JosibQx90G6coyJA10xow/640?wx_fmt=gif" data-type="gif" data-w="400" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">《沁园春·长沙》是毛泽东于1925年晚秋，离开故乡韶山，去广州主持农民运动讲习所的途中，途经长沙，重游橘子洲时所作。其时，作者面对湘江上美丽动人的自然秋景，联想起当时的革命形势，写下了这首词。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.7833333" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKevZbB7CCGibeKgVRtja1EicfFQG5OAYqF0EWLCFD0XPibM1JERIokeCIqvKuzLdG3zMiccHs0CowysBg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="360" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">毛泽东（1893—1976），字润之，湖南湘潭韶山冲（今湖南省韶山市）人，中国共产党、中国人民解放军、中华人民共和国的主要缔造者和领导人，伟大的马克思主义者，无产阶级革命家、战略家、理论家，中国当代杰出的诗人。 </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1893年12月26日生于湖南湘潭韶山冲一个农民家庭。1976年9月9日在北京逝世。中国人民的领袖，马克思主义者，伟大的无产阶级革命家、战略家和理论家，中国共产党、中国人民解放军和中华人民共和国的主要缔造者和领导人，诗人，书法家。中国共产党中央军事委员会主席（1936～1976），中国共产党中央政治局主席（1943～1945）和中央委员会主席（1945～1976），中华人民共和国中央人民政府主席（1949～1954）和中华人民共和国主席（1954～1959）。毛泽东被视为现代世界历史中最重要的人物之一，《时代》杂志也将他评为20世纪最具影响100人之一。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: auto;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);padding-right: 12px;padding-left: 12px;color: rgba(231, 136, 106, 0.62);box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="clear: none;box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Gwen为你</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">读诗</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;float: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;margin-top: -14px;background-color: rgba(231, 136, 106, 0.62);box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us"
